OBJECT Report 16505 Form 26Q
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=03-08-16;
    Time=12:00:00 PM;
    Version List=NAVIN9.00.00.46621;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    CaptionML=[ENU=Form 26Q;
               ENN=Form 26Q];
    OnPreReport=VAR
                  UpdateChallanDetails@1500001 : Report 13721;
                BEGIN
                  CompanyInfo.GET;
                  IF CurrentQuarter = 0 THEN
                    ERROR(Text16500);
                  IF FinancialYear = '' THEN
                    ERROR(Text16501);
                  IF TANLocation = '' THEN
                    ERROR(Text16502);
                  IF PersonName = '' THEN
                    ERROR(Text16503);
                  IF Designation = '' THEN
                    ERROR(Text16504);
                  IF PrintingDate = 0D THEN
                    ERROR(Text16505);
                  IF PANNo = '' THEN
                    ERROR(PANNoEmptyErr);
                  IF CompanyInfo."Phone No." = '' THEN
                    ERROR(CompInfoPhoneNoEmptyErr);
                  IF CompanyInfo."E-Mail" = '' THEN
                    ERROR(CompInfoEmailEmptyErr);
                  IF CompanyInfo."Location Code" = '' THEN
                    ERROR(CompInfoLocationEmptyErr);
                  IF CompanyInfo.Address = '' THEN
                    ERROR(CompInfoAddressEmptyErr);

                  UpdateChallanDetails.UpdateNilChallanEntries(TANLocation,CurrentQuarter,FinancialYear,TRUE);

                  ChallanRegister.RESET;
                  ChallanRegister.SETRANGE("Financial Year",FinancialYear);
                  IF NOT ChallanRegister.FINDFIRST THEN
                    ERROR(Text16506,'Financial Year');
                  ChallanRegister.SETRANGE(Quarter,CurrentQuarter);
                  IF NOT ChallanRegister.FINDFIRST THEN
                    ERROR(Text16506,'Quarter');
                  IF ChallanRegister.FINDFIRST THEN
                    REPEAT
                      IF (ChallanRegister."Challan No." = '') OR ((ChallanRegister."BSR Code" = '') AND
                        (CompanyInfo."Company Status" <> CompanyInfo."Company Status"::Government) AND
                         NOT ChallanRegister."Nil Challan Indicator")
                      THEN
                        ERROR(Text16508);
                      Form26Q27QEntry.RESET;
                      Form26Q27QEntry.SETRANGE("Financial Year",FinancialYear);
                      IF NOT Form26Q27QEntry.FINDFIRST THEN
                        ERROR(Text16506,'Financial Year');
                      Form26Q27QEntry.SETRANGE(Quarter,CurrentQuarter);
                      IF NOT Form26Q27QEntry.FINDFIRST THEN
                        ERROR(Text16506,'Quarter');
                      Form26Q27QEntry.SETRANGE("Form No.",Form26Q27QEntry."Form No."::"26Q");
                      IF NOT Form26Q27QEntry.FINDFIRST THEN
                        ERROR(Text16507);
                      Form26Q27QEntry.SETRANGE("T.A.N. No.",TANLocation);
                      IF NOT Form26Q27QEntry.FINDFIRST THEN
                        ERROR(Text16506,'T.A.N No.');
                      Form26Q27QEntry.SETRANGE(Printed,TRUE);
                      Form26Q27QEntry.SETRANGE("Challan Register Entry No.",ChallanRegister."Entry No.");
                      Execute += Form26Q27QEntry.COUNT;
                    UNTIL ChallanRegister.NEXT=0;

                  IF (CompanyInfo."Company Status" <> CompanyInfo."Company Status"::Government) AND
                    (STRLEN(MobileNo) <> 10)
                  THEN
                    ERROR(Text16520);
                END;

  }
  DATASET
  {
    { 9960;    ;DataItem;                    ;
               DataItemTable=Table16503;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Entry No.)
                                 ORDER(Ascending)
                                 WHERE(Form No.=FILTER(26Q));
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               SETRANGE("Financial Year",FinancialYear);
                               SETRANGE(Quarter,CurrentQuarter);
                               SETRANGE("Form No.","Form No."::"26Q");
                               SETRANGE("Deductor T.A.N. No.",TANLocation);
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  IF Quarter = Quarter::Q4 THEN
                                    Year := COPYSTR(FORMAT("Assessment Year"),1,4)
                                  ELSE
                                    Year := COPYSTR(FORMAT("Financial Year"),1,4);

                                  IF CurrentQuarter = CurrentQuarter::Q1 THEN
                                    MonthText := Text16509
                                  ELSE IF CurrentQuarter = CurrentQuarter::Q2 THEN
                                    MonthText := Text16510
                                  ELSE IF CurrentQuarter = CurrentQuarter::Q3 THEN
                                    MonthText := Text16511
                                  ELSE IF CurrentQuarter = CurrentQuarter::Q4 THEN
                                    MonthText := Text16512;

                                  State.SETFILTER("State Code for eTDS/TCS","Batch Header"."Deductor State");
                                  IF State.FINDFIRST THEN
                                    StateDescription := State.Description;

                                  //IF "Deductor Type" = "Deductor Type"::"0" THEN
                                  //  DeductorType := Text16513;
                                  //IF "Deductor Type" = "Deductor Type"::"1" THEN
                                  //  DeductorType := Text16514;
                                  DeductorType := "Deductor Category";
                                  DeductorCategory.GET("Deductor Category");

                                  IfFiled := Text16515;

                                  IF "Original RRR No." <> '' THEN
                                    IfFiled := Text16516;
                                  Num :=0;
                                END;
                                 }

    { 6267;1   ;DataItem;                    ;
               DataItemTable=Table16505;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Reporting Challan Entry No.,Reporting Quarter,Party Code)
                                 WHERE(Reporting Challan Entry No.=FILTER(<>0),
                                       Form No.=FILTER(26Q));
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               CurrReport.CREATETOTALS("Total TDS Including SHE CESS","TDS Amount",
                                 TotalTaxDeducted,"eCESS Amount","Surcharge Amount","SHE Cess Amount");
                               SETRANGE("T.A.N. No.",TANLocation);
                               SETRANGE(Adjusted,FALSE);
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  NODNOCCertificateNo@1500001 : Record 13784;
                                BEGIN
                                  CertificateNo := '';
                                  Printed := TRUE;
                                  MODIFY;
                                  TotalTDSIncludingeCESS := 0;
                                  Form26Q27QEntry.RESET;
                                  Form26Q27QEntry.SETRANGE("Challan Register Entry No.","Challan Register Entry No.");
                                  IF Form26Q27QEntry.FINDSET THEN
                                    REPEAT
                                      TotalTDSIncludingeCESS += Form26Q27QEntry."Total TDS Including SHE CESS";
                                    UNTIL Form26Q27QEntry.NEXT = 0;

                                  IF CurrentQuarter > 0 THEN BEGIN
                                    TDSAccountingPeriod.SETRANGE("Financial Year for eTDS/TCS",FinancialYear);
                                    IF TDSAccountingPeriod.FINDFIRST THEN
                                      TDSSetup.RESET;
                                    TDSSetup.SETRANGE("No.",TDSAccountingPeriod."No.");
                                    TDSSetup.SETRANGE(Quarter,CurrentQuarter);
                                    IF TDSSetup.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                      EndDate := COPYSTR(FORMAT(TDSSetup."Ending Date"),1,6);
                                      EndDate1 := COPYSTR(FORMAT(TDSSetup."Ending Date"),7,8);
                                    END;
                                  END;

                                  IF "Form 26Q/27Q Entry"."Reporting Challan Entry No." <> OldRepChallanNo THEN BEGIN
                                    Num := 0;
                                    TDSBaseAmt := 0;
                                  END;
                                  OldRepChallanNo := "Form 26Q/27Q Entry"."Reporting Challan Entry No.";
                                  "Challan Register".SETRANGE("Challan No.","Challan No.");
                                  IF "Challan Register".FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                    "Challan Register".CALCFIELDS("Total TDS Including SHE Cess");
                                    AmountAsPerChallan :=
                                      "Challan Register"."Total TDS Including SHE Cess" + "Challan Register"."Oltas Others" +
                                      "Challan Register"."Oltas Interest" + "Challan Register"."TDS Fee";
                                  END;

                                  TotalTaxDeducted := "TDS Amount"+"Surcharge Amount"+"eCESS Amount" + "SHE Cess Amount";

                                  Rate := "TDS %" + ("TDS %" * "Surcharge %" / 100);
                                  RateAtWhichDeducted := Rate + ( Rate * ("eCESS %" + "SHE Cess %") / 100);

                                  Num := Num + 1;
                                  TDSBaseAmt := TDSBaseAmt + ABS("TDS Line Amount");
                                  IF ("Total TDS Including SHE CESS" = 0) AND (NOT "NIL Challan Indicator") THEN
                                    "Concessional Code" := 'Y';

                                  IF "Concessional Code" = '' THEN
                                    "Concessional Code" := Text16517;

                                  NODNOCCertificateNo.SETRANGE("No.","Party Code");
                                  NODNOCCertificateNo.SETFILTER("Stating Date",'<=%1',"Posting Date");
                                  NODNOCCertificateNo.SETFILTER("Ending Date",'>=%1',"Posting Date");
                                  IF NODNOCCertificateNo.FINDFIRST THEN
                                    IF ("Concessional Code" =  'A') OR ("Concessional Code" = 'B') THEN
                                      CertificateNo := NODNOCCertificateNo."Certificate No.";

                                  IF "Deductee Code" = '1' THEN
                                    DeductorCode := Text16518
                                  ELSE
                                    DeductorCode := Text16519;
                                END;

               DataItemLink=Reporting Quarter=FIELD(Quarter),
                            Financial Year=FIELD(Financial Year) }

      { 1500002;2;Field     ;
                  Name=FinancialYear;
                  CaptionML=[ENU=Financial Year;
                             ENN=Financial Year];
                  SourceExpr=FinancialYear;
                  OnLookup=BEGIN
                             IF CurrentQuarter > 0 THEN BEGIN
                               TDSSetup.RESET;
                               TDSSetup.SETRANGE(Quarter,CurrentQuarter);
                               IF TDSSetup.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                 TDSAccountingPeriod.GET(TDSSetup."No.");
                                 IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(PAGE::"Income Tax Accounting Periods",TDSAccountingPeriod) = ACTION::LookupOK THEN
                                   FinancialYear := TDSAccountingPeriod."Financial Year for eTDS/TCS";
                               END;
                             END;
                           END;
                            }

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
